[03/07/2022-05:06:01] [V] === Explanations of the performance metrics ===
[03/07/2022-05:06:01] [V] Total Host Walltime: the host walltime from when the first query (after warmups) is enqueued to when the last query is completed.
[03/07/2022-05:06:01] [V] GPU Compute Time: the GPU latency to execute the kernels for a query.
[03/07/2022-05:06:01] [V] Total GPU Compute Time: the summation of the GPU Compute Time of all the queries. If this is significantly shorter than Total Host Walltime, the GPU may be under-utilized because of host-side overheads or data transfers.
[03/07/2022-05:06:01] [V] Throughput: the observed throughput computed by dividing the number of queries by the Total Host Walltime. If this is significantly lower than the reciprocal of GPU Compute Time, the GPU may be under-utilized because of host-side overheads or data transfers.
[03/07/2022-05:06:01] [V] Enqueue Time: the host latency to enqueue a query. If this is longer than GPU Compute Time, the GPU may be under-utilized.
[03/07/2022-05:06:01] [V] H2D Latency: the latency for host-to-device data transfers for input tensors of a single query.
[03/07/2022-05:06:01] [V] D2H Latency: the latency for device-to-host data transfers for output tensors of a single query.
[03/07/2022-05:06:01] [V] Latency: the summation of H2D Latency, GPU Compute Time, and D2H Latency. This is the latency to infer a single query.
[03/07/2022-05:06:01] [V] End-to-End Host Latency: the duration from when the H2D of a query is called to when the D2H of the same query is completed, which includes the latency to wait for the completion of the previous query. This is the latency of a query if multiple queries are enqueued consecutively.
